# <a name="required-mobile-diagnostic-data-for-microsoft-teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-103">Microsoft Teams 所需的移动设备诊断数据</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-103">Required mobile diagnostic data for Microsoft Teams</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-104">以下文章包含 Microsoft Teams 移动设备事件的列表，以及各个事件收集的属性列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-104">The following article contains a list of Microsoft Teams mobile events, and lists of properties each event collects.</span></span>

## <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-105">事件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-105">Events</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-106">下面列出了所有事件的通用属性，若要评论它们，请参阅[与所有事件一起发送的属性](#properties-sent-with-all-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-106">There are common properties for all events listed below, to review them, see [Properties sent with all events](#properties-sent-with-all-events).</span></span>

### <a name="panelaction"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-107">面板视图</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-107">PanelAction</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-108">关于PanelAction 事件属性的详细信息，请参阅[与面板操作事件一起发送的属性](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-108">For information on the properties of PanelAction events, see [Properties sent with panelaction events](#properties-sent-with-panelaction-events).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - 当用户切换辅助功能时。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-109">**accessibilityUserConfiguration** - When a users toggles an accessibility feature.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - 在“我们已更新通知设置”对话框中确认更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-110">**acknowledgeSettingChange** - Acknowledge an update in the we updated a notification setting dialog.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-111">这是一个用于确认更新通知和确定整体通知可靠性的功能成功指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-111">This is a feature success metrics used to acknowledge update notifications and to determine overall notification reliability.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-112">**actionComposeMenu**</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-113">创建邮件扩展使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-113">Create message extension usage.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-114">行动消息扩展使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-114">Action message extension usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - 已取消位置共享可用提醒横幅。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-115">**active_session_banner_dismissed** - The location sharing active reminder banner was dismissed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-116">**activityChatClicked** - 在“**活动**”选项卡中选择非实时聊天或显示拆分视图时触发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-116">**activityChatClicked** - Triggered when non-live chat is selected in the **Activity** tab or a split view is shown.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-117">**activityContextMenu** - 活动源中的溢出操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-117">**activityContextMenu** - Overflow actions in the activity feed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-118">**activityFeedClick** - 点击了活动源项，并导航到了机器人聊天。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-118">**activityFeedClick** - An activity feed item is tapped on and a bot chat is navigated to.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - 捕获订阅源项目上的长按手势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-119">**activityFeedLongPress** - Captures long press gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - 捕获订阅源项目上的轻扫手势。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-120">**activityFeedSwipe** - Captures swipe gestures on feed items.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-121">**activityFilterClick** - 捕获活动筛选器使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-121">**activityFilterClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - 捕获活动筛选器使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-122">**activityFilterOptionsClick** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - 捕获活动筛选器使用情况。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-123">**activityFilterOptionsClicked** - Captures activity filter usage.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - 从“**活动**”选项卡上的实时会议中选择聊天时触发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-124">**activityLiveChatClicked** - Triggered when chat is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - 当从“**活动**”选项卡上的实时会议中选择“**详细信息**”时触发。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-125">**activityLiveDetailsClicked** - Triggered when **Details** is selected from a live meeting on the **Activity** tab.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-126">**activityTabClicked** - 有助于确定：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-126">**activityTabClicked** - Helps to determine if:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-127">显示“**活动**”选项卡。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-127">The **Activity** tab is shown.</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-128">Teams 捕获“**活动**”选项卡事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-128">Teams captures an **Activity** tab event.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - 捕获活动筛选器使用情况，以在“**我的活动**”和“**源**”之间切换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-129">**activityTypeDropdown** - Captures activity filter usage to switch between **My Activity** and **Feeds**.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-130">**addChannel** - 添加频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-130">**addChannel** - Adding a channel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-131">此项提供有关成功创建频道的成功数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-131">This item provides success data around the successful creation of a channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-132">**addMember**- 已在“**更多**”菜单中选中并触发了“**邀请他人**”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-132">**addMember** - Triggered the **Invite people** button is selected in the **More** menu.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-133">**addMembers** - 将成员添加到团队或专用频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-133">**addMembers** - Add members to a team or private channel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-134">**addToCalendar** - 为“专用日历”中缺少的日历事件选择“**添加到日历**”按钮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-134">**addToCalendar** - Select the **Add to calendar** button for calendar events missing in private calendar.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-135">**addToList** - 已将联系人添加到联系人列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-135">**addToList** - A contact is added to a contact list.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-136">**addToMeeting** - 在会议的参与者列表中，选择“**添加到会议**”按钮（适用于聊天的参与者）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-136">**addToMeeting** - Select the **Add to meeting** button in the participant list for a meeting (for participants who are a part of the chat).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-137">**addUserAsContact** - 可通过从联系人的个人资料卡片中选择“**添加联系人**”图标来添加联系人。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-137">**addUserAsContact** - A contact can be added by selecting the **Add contact** icon from the profile card of the contact.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-138">**admitAll** - 从“大厅”一节选择“**全部允许**”按钮的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-138">**admitAll** - The number of times the **Admit all** button is selected from the lobby section.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-139">**admitParticipant** - 从会议名单中允许某人参加会议的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-139">**admitParticipant** - The number of times someone is admitted into a meeting from the meeting roster.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-140">**alertsNavAlert** - 点击源项目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-140">**alertsNavAlert** - Tapping on a feed item.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-141">**android: null** - 聊天机器人静音或取消静音。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-141">**android: null** - Mute or unmute a bot chat.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-142">这正增强只添加应用程序信息聊天的现有遥测。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-142">This is enhancing existing telemetry around chats only adds application information.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-143">**anonymousMeetingJoin** - 在匿名加入提供名称页上选择“**加入会议**”或在“名称”对话框中单击“**确定**”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-143">**anonymousMeetingJoin** - **Join meeting** is selected on an anonymous join provide name page or **OK** is tapped in the name dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-147">**anonymousMeetingSignIn** - 用户从名称输入屏幕导航到登录的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-147">**anonymousMeetingSignIn** - The number of times a user navigated to sign-in from the name input screen.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-149">**anonymousMeetingToggleMuted** - 选择“静音”切换按钮的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-149">**anonymousMeetingToggleMuted** - The number of times the mute toggle button was selected.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-159">**audioOnlyLowBatteryBanner** - 由于电池电量不足，选择了“**仅音频**”选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-159">**audioOnlyLowBatteryBanner** - The **Audio only** option is selected due to a low battery banner.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-162">**autoReconnectCallmebackCallDrop** - 在呼叫结束屏幕上选择 **Callmeback** 按钮的次数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-162">**autoReconnectCallmebackCallDrop** - The number of times the **Callmeback** button was selected at a call end screen.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-163">**autoReconnectDialIn**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-163">**autoReconnectDialIn**</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-173">**blockAnonymous** - 时间：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-173">**blockAnonymous** - When:</span></span>
  - <span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-174">启用通话设置以从设置中阻止没有来电显示的呼叫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-174">Enables calling setting to block calls without caller id from settings.</span></span>

### <a name="scenario"></a><span data-ttu-id="0b4ab-1300">使用场景</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="0b4ab-1300">Scenario</span></span>
